Evaluating Step 0 by human...
LLM Evaluation: 1. Yes.
2. Reason: The human's statement contains an error in the translation process. The sentence "I like apples" should be translated into Tizin following the structure of Verb-Object-Subject. The human correctly identifies that the verb "Maktay" (indicating an intense like) should come first, and "Apple" should be the direct object. However, they have used "Mato" instead of "Pa" for the subject "I." Since "Pa" is the nominative form indicating oneself and should be used as the subject in this sentence, the correct translation should be "Maktay apple Pa" instead of "Maktay mato apple."
